`GenerateCredentialsAsync()`\n- Falls back to synchronous `GenerateCredentials()` if async fails\n- Invokes `UpdateCache()` to store credentials based on authenticator flags\n\n**UpdateCache** attributes\n\n## Challenge Selection and Processing\n\n**GetCredentials** implements challenge prioritization:\n- Parses multiple authentication schemes using `ChallengeParser`\n- Ranks schemes by strength (Negotiate > NTLM > Digest > Basic)\n- Selects the first supported authenticator that succeeds\n\n**PromptForIdentity** handles user interaction:\n- Presents credential dialogs when cached credentials fail\n- Respects cross-origin and subresource restrictions via `BlockPrompt()`\n- Tracks authentication attempts to warn users of failures\n\n## Asynchronous Flow Management\n\n**OnAuthAvailable** processes user-provided credentials:\n- Receives credentials from async prompt callbacks\n- Generates final credentials through the selected authenticator\n- Continues request processing via `ContinueOnAuthAvailable()`\n\n**OnCredsGenerated** handles async credential generation completion:\n- Updates continuation state for multi-round authentication (NTLM,
